<tr><td VALIGN=TOP width="626"><h2 align=center>中医推荐“养脾胃三宝”摆脱疲劳、胃病又降压</h2>
<img width="600" src="https://i.epochtimes.com/assets/uploads/2020/08/pumpkin_378719704.jpg" class="" data-thumbnail="true" />
<h6></h6>
<hr></p><div><figure style="max-width:640px" class="aligncenter"><ahref="https://i.epochtimes.com/assets/uploads/2018/11/shutterstock_1113050384.jpg" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer"><picture><source srcSet="/_next/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fi.epochtimes.com%2Fassets%2Fuploads%2F2018%2F11%2Fshutterstock_1113050384.jpg&amp;w=1200&amp;q=75" type="image/webp"/><source srcSet="https://i.epochtimes.com/assets/uploads/2018/11/shutterstock_1113050384.jpg" type="image/jpeg"/><img src="/_next/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fi.epochtimes.com%2Fassets%2Fuploads%2F2018%2F11%2Fshutterstock_1113050384.jpg&amp;w=1200&amp;q=75" alt="山药能补脾胃、益肾气、化痰涎、润皮毛。(Shutterstock)" width="640" b="auto"/></picture></a><figcaption>山药能补脾胃、益肾气、化痰涎、润皮毛。(Shutterstock)</figcaption></figure></div><p>中药房卖的山药，是晒干了的；而新鲜的山药很漂亮，切开后白白黏黏的，生吃、熟吃都可以。</p><p>山药能补脾胃、益肾气、化痰涎、润皮毛。脾胃虚弱的人容易身体疲倦、消化不良，可以吃山药来增强体力；对于十几岁的孩子，则有助长高发育。脾养好皮肤也会变得红润，所以吃山药也能滋润皮肤。</p><div class=" lg:hidden"><div class="m-auto flex items-center justify-center overflow-hidden print:hidden" style="min-height:266px;padding:8px 8px 8px 8px" data-testid="ad-container-DJY_M_article_336x280_2"><div id="DJY_M_article_336x280_2"></div></div></div><p>山药还有降低血糖的功效。想要避免血糖过高的人，可以吃“山药排骨汤”，排骨本身含有胶质和钙质，两种食材一起炖煮对身体非常有益。“四神汤”是人们耳熟能详的补脾胃药膳，其中也有山药，炖煮时可以多放一些，以改善高血糖的问题。</p><div class="hidden lg:block"><div class="m-auto items-center justify-center overflow-hidden print:hidden hidden md:flex" style="min-height:266px;padding:8px 8px 8px 8px" data-testid="ad-container-DJY_D_article_300x250_1"><div id="DJY_D_article_300x250_1"></div></div></div><p>除此之外，山药又能补肾，使人精力旺盛，读书专注，耳聪目明。</p><h3>2. 第二宝南瓜 改善胃痛、胃病</h3><div><figure style="max-width:640px" class="aligncenter"><ahref="https://i.epochtimes.com/assets/uploads/2018/01/nangua.jpg" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer"><picture><source srcSet="/_next/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fi.epochtimes.com%2Fassets%2Fuploads%2F2018%2F01%2Fnangua.jpg&amp;w=1200&amp;q=75" type="image/webp"/><source srcSet="https://i.epochtimes.com/assets/uploads/2018/01/nangua.jpg" type="image/jpeg"/><img src="/_next/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fi.epochtimes.com%2Fassets%2Fuploads%2F2018%2F01%2Fnangua.jpg&amp;w=1200&amp;q=75" alt="南瓜是健胃消食的好食物，可以补脾、增进食欲、改善胃痛。(Shutterstock)" width="640" b="auto"/></picture></a><figcaption>南瓜是健胃消食的好食物，可以补脾、增进食欲、改善胃痛。(Shutterstock)</figcaption></figure></div><p>南瓜是健胃消食的好食物，可以补脾、增进食欲、改善胃痛。凡是患有胃痛的人，吃些南瓜，都会觉得比较舒服。从营养学角度来说，南瓜含丰富的果胶，能够保护胃黏膜，预防胃炎、胃溃疡等问题。（推荐阅读：<span style="text-decoration:underline"><span style="color:#188638"><a style="color:#188638;text-decoration:underline" href="https://www.epochtimes.com/b5/18/1/27/n10092467.md#1" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer nofollow" target="_blank" class="health-article-hover-class">南瓜是天然的“免疫增强剂” 还能降三高</a></span></span>）</p><p>工作压力大、常常胃痛的人，往往是因为吃饭时间不固定。如果实在难以规律三餐，建议一个礼拜吃一、两次南瓜粥或南瓜来养胃。</p><p>南瓜的叶、籽都是宝。有一次我到美国北卡罗莱纳州见朋友，他家的园子种植南瓜，当时正是春夏之交，南瓜叶长得很漂亮，他剪下南瓜叶，炒了一盘菜，好吃又美味。</p><div class=" lg:hidden"><div class="m-auto flex items-center justify-center overflow-hidden print:hidden" style="min-height:266px;padding:8px 8px 8px 8px" data-testid="ad-container-DJY_M_article_336x280_3"><div id="DJY_M_article_336x280_3"></div></div></div><p>南瓜田里的农夫不容易得摄护腺肥大的疾病，这可能与他们常吃南瓜和南瓜子有关。南瓜子含锌，对摄护腺有益。</p><p>以前我在当兵和读大学的时候，餐厅里的伙食常有粉蒸肉，肉底下就会铺南瓜或地瓜。假如喜欢自己做饭吃，可以这样做试试看，既好吃又养生。</p><h3>3. 第三宝地瓜 增强体力、降压排毒</h3><div><figure style="max-width:640px" class="aligncenter"><ahref="https://i.epochtimes.com/assets/uploads/2019/01/sweet-potato.jpg" target="_blank" rel="noopener noreferrer"><picture><source srcSet="/_next/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fi.epochtimes.com%2Fassets%2Fuploads%2F2019%2F01%2Fsweet-potato.jpg&amp;w=1200&amp;q=75" type="image/webp"/><source srcSet="https://i.epochtimes.com/assets/uploads/2019/01/sweet-potato.jpg" type="image/jpeg"/><img src="/_next/image?url=https%3A%2F%2Fi.epochtimes.com%2Fassets%2Fuploads%2F2019%2F01%2Fsweet-potato.jpg&amp;w=1200&amp;q=75" alt="地瓜又称为红薯、番薯，能益气生津，补脾虚、宽肠胃、通便秘。(Shutterstock)" width="640" b="auto"/></picture></a><figcaption>地瓜又称为红薯、番薯，能益气生津，补脾虚、宽肠胃、通便秘。(Shutterstock)</figcaption></figure></div><p>地瓜又称为红薯、番薯，能益气生津，补脾虚、宽肠胃、通便秘。老年人他吃不下东西的时候，不妨给他煮一碗地瓜粥，帮助养脾胃、增强体力。</p><div class="hidden lg:block"><div class="m-auto items-center justify-center overflow-hidden print:hidden hidden md:flex" style="min-height:266px;padding:8px 8px 8px 8px" data-testid="ad-container-DJY_D_article_300x250_3"><div id="DJY_D_article_300x250_3"></div></div></div><p>常常吃地瓜的人，排气、排便比较顺畅，而且可以改善大部分的肠道疾病。</p><p></p><p>要降脾胃火，有一个最简单的办法，就是吃些比较寒凉的食物，譬如莲藕。莲藕粉、莲藕茶都可以。西瓜也不错，又称“先天白虎汤”，在夏天吃，能帮助降温降火气。</p><div class=" lg:hidden"><div class="m-auto flex items-center justify-center overflow-hidden print:hidden" style="min-height:266px;padding:8px 8px 8px 8px" data-testid="ad-container-DJY_M_article_336x280_4"><div id="DJY_M_article_336x280_4"></div></div></div><p></p><p></p></div><div class="mt-6 space-y-2 text-base lg:px-10"><div class="flex flex-row items-start gap-2"><div class="text-gray-90 my-1 whitespace-nowrap">標籤</div><div class="flex flex-wrap items-center "><span class="m-1 rounded-full border px-2 text-zinc-500"><ahref="/gb/tag/健脾.md#1" class="hover:text-[#0066B3]" target="_self">健脾</a></span><span class="m-1 rounded-full border px-2 text-zinc-500"><ahref="/gb/tag/南瓜.md#1" class="hover:text-[#0066B3]" target="_self">南瓜</a></span><span class="m-1 rounded-full border px-2 text-zinc-500"><ahref="/gb/tag/地瓜.md#1" class="hover:text-[#0066B3]" target="_self">地瓜</a></span><span class="m-1 rounded-full border px-2 text-zinc-500"><ahref="/gb/tag/山药.md#1" class="hover:text-[#0066B3]" target="_self">山药</a></span><span class="m-1 rounded-full border px-2 text-zinc-500"><ahref="/gb/tag/消化.md#1" class="hover:text-[#0066B3]"
